  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_dbd0737f-db5a-4940-b417-927be9c0ccfa'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer7643885983621547288">Tras la muerte de su padre, el prestigioso empresario alemán Eric Zimmerman decide viajar a España para supervisar las delegaciones de la empresa Müller. En la oficina central de Madrid conoce a Judith, una joven ingeniosa y simpática de la que se encapricha de inmediato.<br/><br/>Judith sucumbe a la atracción que el alemán ejerce sobre ella y acepta formar parte de sus juegos sexua</span>
  <span id="freeText7643885983621547288" style="display:none">Tras la muerte de su padre, el prestigioso empresario alemán Eric Zimmerman decide viajar a España para supervisar las delegaciones de la empresa Müller. En la oficina central de Madrid conoce a Judith, una joven ingeniosa y simpática de la que se encapricha de inmediato.<br /><br />Judith sucumbe a la atracción que el alemán ejerce sobre ella y acepta formar parte de sus juegos sexuales, repletos de fantasías y erotismo. Junto a él aprenderá que todos llevamos dentro un voyeur, y que las personas se dividen en sumisas y dominantes... Pero el tiempo pasa, la relación se intensifica y Eric empieza a temer que se descubra su secreto, algo que podría marcar el principio o el fin de la relación.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2204688403?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nikki (Saturday Nite Reader)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nikki (Saturday Nite Reader)" href="/user/show/1347292-nikki-saturday-nite-reader">Nikki (Saturday Nite Reader)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/35175432-tell-me-what-you-want">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1347292-nikki-saturday-nite-reader?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2204688403" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14186481121062731223">I won this in a goodreads giveaway and didn’t know what to fully expect. Nevermind that it was playing off of 50 Shades (which isn’t a literary work either) but this was just not for me. I can get passed the sexual choices (a bit too brazen for me though, not my thing), but I was not a fan of the weak main character who made excuse after excuse because she thought she was in love (like after a few romps and knowing he isn’t only with her). I don’t know why I kept reading, maybe to see how this w</span>
  <span id="freeText14186481121062731223" style="display:none">I won this in a goodreads giveaway and didn’t know what to fully expect. Nevermind that it was playing off of 50 Shades (which isn’t a literary work either) but this was just not for me. I can get passed the sexual choices (a bit too brazen for me though, not my thing), but I was not a fan of the weak main character who made excuse after excuse because she thought she was in love (like after a few romps and knowing he isn’t only with her). I don’t know why I kept reading, maybe to see how this would end and than that ending (but really, what did I expect?) <br /><br />I am more mad at myself for not putting this in my DNF pile. Stay clear of this one.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14186481121062731223" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText15543303902689446946" style="display:none">In all honesty, I was completely shocked by how good this book was. I'm normally not into the whole sex from the start, however, this book completely changed my mind.<br /><br />I love Jude as a character, she's bold, stubborn, doesn't take crap from anyone, and she's a dare devil. Eric was your normal boss type of character, but he had his own unique personality when it came to certain things. For instance, you see the worry and love in his words even before he really knew what was happening. The only thing I didn't care for about Eric as a character was how much he had moodswings. I know he had his reasons but it would have definitely pushed me away.<br /><br />All in all, I think this was a great book with a lot of erotica. I would recommend this book to anyone that enjoys erotica and I can't wait to read the second book when it comes out.</span>

  <span id="freeText13780569816928521422" style="display:none">Thank you, Net Galley for the opportunity to review this book --- as people who follow me know, I do not regurgitate what the book is about as that is usually evident from the title and book jacket and what the description from the top of the page where my reviews end up (Amazon, Goodreads, etc.) HOWEVER … as this is a fiction book that I have reviewed that is not necessarily obvious or self-explanatory from the title do here is what was provided by the publisher!<br /><br />Getting stuck in an elevator with a flirtatious and charismatic stranger leaves Jude Flores flustered enough—even before she realizes that he’s Eric Zimmerman, the powerful billionaire CEO…and her powerfully sexy new boss.Having arrived in Spain to take over his company’s office, Eric is clearly interested in more than business. He notices Jude for her brilliance and talent, but it’s her humility that excites him the most.<br />Seduced by Eric’s attention, Jude accepts his bold invitation into his private life and a world of pleasure she’d only fantasized about. With each clandestine meeting comes Eric’s desire to push further. And before long, Jude is falling—helplessly, willingly, and without inhibition. But as their relationship deepens, Jude begins to wonder what other secrets Eric is hiding behind that sexy smile—and how far she’s willing to go to find out.<br /><br />What can you expect from a book that starts with someone stuck in their car while their supervisor has sex on the car next to them in the parking garage? Sex. sex. and more sex. Billionaire bosses books are left, right, and center these days and if this is your forte, this is the book for you! Escapist, downright silly at times but on a cold, rainy, windy day like today when snow is in the forecast? Enjoyable. </span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yZC2Epk9sQNCmLgE/jjcz2M04GON8yaVXNxHuwpwO03Nk3oBV+VNDQNqbeMt9QMlQMzyaXkwTGzeSSm3olixqw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('iGh1JuH/rbcr+3beP/CfTgdRZj1NPj7Leym/jdhO4jCMa7k1LydRuWoJoznsPUCkJKl0N7n9VDL5vNGBcGZo1g==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13422814643797882517">María del Carmen Rodríguez del Álamo Lázaro was born on 1965 in Nuremberg, Germany, daugther of a Spanish mother and a North American father. She grew up in Madrid, Spain. She worked during years as secretary. Under the pseudonym of Megan Maxwell (her first heroine), she published romance novels since 2010.</span>

            <span class="readable">&ldquo;-¿Sale a cenar con muchos hombres?<br />Aquella pregunta me sorprende. Pero ¿este tío se cree el único espécimen macho del mundo? Así que respiro hondo y procuro no soltarle un borderío de los míos.<br />-Siempre que me apetece –le aclaro.<br />Alzo mi barbilla con altanería y, cuando creo que no voy a decir ni una palabra más, le suelto:<br />-Lo que no entiendo es qué hago aquí, en su coche, con usted y dirigiéndome a cenar. Eso es lo que todavía no logro entender.<br />Él no responde. Sólo me mira… me mira… me mira y me pone histérica con su mirada.<br />-¿Va usted a hablar o pretende estar el resto del viaje mirándome?<br />-Mirarla es muy agradable, señorita Flores.&rdquo;</span>
